@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

#### Titular Empires #####
e_roman_empire = {
	color = { 167 10 100 }
	color2 = { 255 255 20 }
	capital = c_roma # Rome
	
	definite_form = yes
	
	#Always for greeks and latins
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = culture_group:latin_group
					culture_group = culture_group:byzantine_group
				}
			}
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
	
	cultural_names = {
		#Roman Cultures
		roman = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_gallic = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_hispanic = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_british = cn_imperium_romanum
		african_romance = cn_imperium_romanum
		raetoroman = cn_imperium_romanum
		thraco_roman = cn_imperium_romanum
		illyro_roman = cn_imperium_romanum
		pannonian = cn_imperium_romanum
		dalmatian = cn_imperium_romanum
		noricroman = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_gothic = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_dacian = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_frank = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_aramean = cn_imperium_romanum
		romano_vandalic = cn_imperium_romanum
		#Byzantine Cultures
		greek = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		aeolian = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		helleno_aramean = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		greek_gothic = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		greek_persian = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		isaurian_persian = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		grecco_axumite = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		bosporan = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		pontic = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		tsakonian = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		massalian = cn_basileia_rhomaion
		helleno_thracian = cn_basileia_rhomaion
	}
	
	#Should be creatable by decision
	can_create = { always = no }
}

e_wre = {
	color={ 220 20 60 }
	color2 = { 255 255 20 }
	capital = c_ravenna
	
	definite_form = yes
	
	#Correct Title for Latins
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture_group = culture_group:latin_group }
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
	
	#Should be creatable by decision
	can_create = { always = no }
}

	k_annonaria = {
		color={ 220 20 60 }
		capital = c_ravenna
		
		#Keep the ostrogoths et al. from changing away from k_italy
		can_create = {
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NAND = {
					culture = ostrogothic
					culture = skirian
					culture = heruli
					culture = romano_gothic
					has_landed_title = k_ostrogoths
				}
				AND = {
					highest_held_title_tier > tier_kingdom
					OR = {
						culture = ostrogothic
						culture = skirian
						culture = romano_gothic
					}
				}
			}
		}

	k_italia = {
		color={ 178 34 34 }
		capital = c_roma
		
		# Creation trigger
		can_create = { #Keeps the Ostrogoths from changing from k_italy
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NAND = {
					culture = ostrogothic
					culture = skirian
					culture = heruli
					culture = romano_gothic
					has_landed_title = k_ostrogoths
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {

		color={ 180 80 80 }
		capital = c_cetina
		
		# Creation trigger
		can_create = { #Keeps the Ostrogoths from changing from k_italy
			OR = {
				ai = no
				NAND = {
					culture = ostrogothic
					culture = skirian
					culture = heruli
					culture = romano_gothic
					has_landed_title = k_ostrogoths
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
						culture = ostrogothic
						culture = skirian
						culture = heruli
						culture = romano_gothic
					}
				}
			}
		}

				OR = {
					ai = no
					NAND = {
						culture = ostrogothic
						culture = skirian
						culture = heruli
						culture = romano_gothic
						has_landed_title = k_ostrogoths
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
							culture = ostrogothic
							culture = skirian
							culture = heruli
							culture = romano_gothic
						}
					}
				}

#### Other Roman-associated Titles ####
k_italy = {
	color = { 244 227 160 }
	color2 = { 255 255 255 }
	capital = c_lombardia # Pavia
	
	can_create = {
		trigger_if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			faith = { religion_tag = christianity_religion }
		}
	}
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = culture:italian }
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
}

d_italy_prefect = {
	color = { 200 150 43 }
	color2 = { 0 128 128 }
	capital = c_ravenna # Ravenna
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		#ai never change title
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
	
	can_create = { always = no }
}

	ai_primary_priority = {
		#ai never change title
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}

}

k_republic = {
	color = { 173 0 0 }
	capital = c_roma # Rome
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		#ai never change title
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
	
	# Creation/Usurp Trigger
	can_create = {
		has_culture = culture:roman
		age = 25
		has_government = republic_government
		prestige = 200
		independent = yes
		realm_size = 50
	}
}
